Current Commentary

Exhortation to Representative Shi 18

Representative Shi has wired his resignation, citing the increasingly difficult diplomatic situation and the incompatibility of diplomatic policy with public opinion. This news has shocked us and deepened our sense of the difficulty of justice prevailing over violence. The League of Nations has failed to uphold the sanctity of its covenant, further endangering the Far East.

Representative Shi was entrusted by our nation and its people to attend the League of Nations and negotiate on our behalf. For the past seventy days, he has fought alone, enduring hardships and demonstrating exceptional ability, which has been admired by the Chinese people. Today, although justice is declining and the future is fraught with danger, leading to extreme difficulties in coping, resulting in a pessimistic attitude, this is human nature and deserves our deep sympathy. However, on the day when the nation is facing difficulties, the only responsibility of the people is to strive forward, not to be passive, but to overcome obstacles and advance, never to shrink from difficulties and shirk responsibility. Therefore, at this critical moment, the people entrust the life of the nation and the race entirely to Representative Shi. Since Representative Shi has undertaken this heavy task, there is no justification for resignation at this time.

We truly know that today justice has been submerged by violence, and that the League of Nations has in fact succumbed to Japan. We share the eternal sorrow of weak nations having no diplomacy. However, with a firm stance and based on established facts, we must loudly proclaim to the world and fight to the death against violence, so that the world knows that justice can be hijacked by violence, but it cannot be subjugated by violence. The Chinese nation still possesses an indomitable spirit.

Furthermore, the only backing for diplomacy is public sentiment. Today, public sentiment in our country is remarkably unified. The insistence that there be no negotiations with Japan until its troops are withdrawn is unanimous and unwavering. This firm and fervent public sentiment is a powerful support for diplomacy. Representative Shi must pay attention to accepting and upholding the public opinion of the people in determining the direction of diplomatic negotiations. Diplomacy may fail, but the principle must be consistently upheld. The boiling blood of the Chinese people today will not allow Representative Shi to be trapped in a lonely struggle. If Representative Shi resigns because the principle cannot be upheld, then the resignation has meaning. But if he resigns because the environment is difficult, then the resignation is a shirking of responsibility, a betrayal of the nation and its people.

General Zhan Shan, the solitary army in the isolated region of Heilongjiang, has been fighting against the violent army from beginning to end. Despite the defeat at Qiqihar, he is still making persistent efforts, undaunted and unyielding, and is actively preparing to counterattack and recover the lost territory. We sincerely hope that Representative Shi will also maintain this attitude of responsibility and perseverance. We dare to tell Representative Shi that the people of our country are now prepared to fight to the death for the survival of the nation. When diplomacy reaches the point where no concessions can be made, it will be the time for the final struggle of our people, and we will never allow the responsible representative to be trapped in a lonely struggle. Representative Shi, strive forward!

Domestic Important Telegrams Two

Ministry of Propaganda Hosts News Reporters 19

Chen Bulei Grieves Over Student Actions

Cheng Tianfang Reports on Recent Diplomacy

(Nanjing) The Central Propaganda Department hosted the news media at the second conference hall of the Central Party Headquarters at 3:00 PM on the 6th. About 50 reporters from various newspapers, news agencies, and resident reporters from other places attended the meeting. Chen Bulei and Cheng Tianfang, the two ministers of the Central Propaganda Department, as well as secretaries Zhu Yunguang and Fang Zhi, were present. After Chen Bulei, the chairman, respectfully read the Premier's will, he reported on the recent situation of students petitioning in Nanjing. (1) The Central Government's policy toward the student movement is entirely based on the attitude of parents and elder brothers towards their children, cherishing them from beginning to end and never abandoning the responsibility of discipline. As for national laws and social order, we will certainly maintain them with all our strength. This is the consistent attitude of the government. (2) On the 5th, a portion of the Peking University demonstration group was sent to Xiaolingwei for temporary residence. The government's intention was to temporarily isolate them, like parents disciplining their children, to prevent their actions from affecting other children. This is because the various remarks and actions expressed by the group after arriving in Nanjing were completely different from those of previous students who had come to Nanjing to petition. However, the government did not conduct a serious interrogation of them. On the one hand, their food, clothing, and shelter were taken care of as usual. On the other hand, President Jiang Menglin was urgently telegraphed to come to Nanjing to lead them back to school. However, President Jiang telegraphed back that he was temporarily unable to come to Nanjing. The authorities, believing that the students should not neglect their studies for too long, prepared vehicles for them on the evening of the 5th to send them north, but it is heard that they have not yet departed. (3) Recently, students from various places have shown signs of unrest. This may be due to diplomatic tensions, but the government has clearly announced its policy. The doubts caused by previous internal and external misinformation should be swept away. How could the National Government under the guidance of the Kuomintang of China commit any act of national humiliation or betrayal that would lead to its own demise? The various expressions of students from various places seem to suggest that under the name of patriotism, anything can be done. This painful phenomenon is the result of decades of maleducation and cannot be blamed on anyone, but we cannot shirk the responsibility of correcting it. When young people's emotions are agitated, their thinking becomes simpler and simpler. They often only care about actions and forget their goals, completely ignoring the seriousness of the results of their actions. For example, the purpose of expressing the patriotic movement is nothing more than to deal with foreign countries, but as in the recent phenomenon, students stay in school but do not attend classes, and even beat people at will. In Beiping, Jinan, and other places, students demand vehicles to go south and refuse to leave the station, disrupting transportation on the Pingpu Railway. Will such phenomena not cause the enemy to laugh at us for having domestic order in chaos before foreign aggression? What benefit will such a way of loving the country bring to the country? The misuse of young people's energy is the greatest loss to the country. It is hoped that the media will implement the responsibility of guidance and promote the self-awareness of young people, etc. Next, Cheng Tianfang reported on recent diplomacy, briefly stating that in the past week, the atmosphere of the League of Nations and the attention of all parties in the country have been focused on China's three issues: one is the issue of establishing a buffer zone in Jinzhou, the second is the Tianjin incident, and the third is direct negotiations between China and Japan. The course of these three events has been seen in the talks and statements by responsible parties published in various newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai on the 5th, and the truth can be made clear. What we should know is that Jinzhou is the location of the temporary government of Liaoning Province, and Tianjin is the location of the government of Hebei Province. Their status is not just that of ordinary cities. The government cannot easily withdraw and hand over the central枢紐 of a province's government decrees. If Jinzhou and Tianjin are attacked, the government has the determination to resist and defend itself. This can be responsibly told to everyone. As for the claim of direct negotiations, it is because Japanese Minister Shigemitsu came to Nanjing to congratulate Minister Gu and had two meetings with him, leading to speculation that China and Japan had begun negotiations. We believe that under the current National Government, there is no possibility of secret direct negotiations to resolve the Sino-Japanese issue. You can also rest assured about this. The League of Nations has been in session for three weeks, and a new resolution has been drafted. The most important points are three: (1) The resolution of September 30 remains in effect; (2) Five inspectors from neutral countries are sent to Northeast China for inspection; (3) Another meeting will be held on January 25 next year, but the chairman is requested to pay attention to the issue of Northeast China at any time and may convene a meeting in advance if necessary. In addition, there are two points worth noting in the introduction by Chairman Briand: (1) It is hoped that Japan will quickly fulfill the resolution of September 30 and withdraw its troops to the railway zone; (2) A small number of bandits in Northeast China are endangering the lives and property of the local people (including Japanese residents). Before the withdrawal of Japanese troops, they may take police measures when necessary to protect the safety of Japanese residents. This resolution has neither clearly stipulated the deadline for Japan's withdrawal nor recognized the Japanese army's right to suppress bandits, which is not satisfactory to the Chinese people. The government and Representative Shi are still fighting for it, and the Japanese side is not satisfied with the new resolution either. They believe that the resolution of September 30 should not be mentioned again, and that Japan should not only have police measures but also require the right to military action. Therefore, whether this resolution can be passed unanimously is still a question. However, the government has made up its mind to resist Japan's violence and will never give in. Although the League of Nations seems to be softening its attitude, Japan's unreasonable behavior is causing the world to take notice, which may not be beneficial to Japan in the end. Germany before the European War can serve as a warning to Japan. It is hoped that the country will achieve unity, that the people will trust the government, that there will be no unnecessary disputes, and that efforts will be made to prepare for external resistance. It is especially hoped that the press will uphold justice and lead the people to this goal. The meeting was adjourned after the report. (6th Central News Agency dispatch)

Japanese Exert Efforts to Purchase Our Country's Currency 25

Large Quantities of Silver Dollars Shipped to Dalian

(Nanjing) Banking circles have learned that Japanese merchants are secretly purchasing our country's currency in Shanghai, Hankou, and other ports in an attempt to shake the monetary system. Although the Ministry of Finance has issued orders prohibiting the export of silver, their conspiracies and tricks are difficult to prevent. On the morning of the 4th, a Japanese ship arrived in Dalian from Shanghai, carrying 50 boxes of our country's currency, each box containing 30,000 yuan, totaling 1.5 million yuan. The Japanese authorities in charge of the port secretly ordered all parties and the press not to disclose this matter, under penalty of severe punishment. Therefore, few people outside know about it (6th dispatch)

(Nanjing) Financial circles have learned that since the Northeast Incident, the price of Japanese gold notes in China has plummeted, and the losses have been enormous due to the falling price of gold worldwide. Moreover, Chinese merchants refuse to accept them when purchasing raw materials and goods, so they are using the depreciated gold notes to purchase large quantities of Chinese silver dollars and are broadly purchasing banknotes from various banks, using the banknotes to absorb raw materials. Their purpose is to: 1. Completely flood the Chinese market with banknotes from Chinese banks; 2. Completely absorb Chinese silver dollars into Japanese financial institutions, making it impossible for Japan to use gold notes to purchase large quantities of raw materials and cash. It is reported that all silver coin merchants in the country are paying close attention to this matter (6th dispatch)

Japanese Retired Soldiers Raise Funds to Manufacture Military Aircraft 26

Sendai Division Transferred to Northeast China

The Domon Division, originally stationed in Miyagi Prefecture, Japan, is now striving in Manchuria and Mongolia. This afternoon, the Miyagi Prefecture Veterans Branch held a special meeting to hold a launching ceremony for the "Miyagino" (name of a heavy bomber) and resolved to collect 200,000 yuan from veteran members across the country by February 20 next year to manufacture an aircraft. After completion, it will be sent to Manchuria to the front line of national defense (6th Japan United News Agency dispatch)

The Japanese Ministry of War dispatched Major Yanagida of the Army Ministry's Military Affairs Bureau to Sendai due to the severe cold in northern Manchuria. This morning at 7:00 AM, Yanagida went to the Second Division Garrison Headquarters to attend a cadre meeting. As a result, it was decided to send two battalions of soldiers under the jurisdiction of the Second Division Headquarters to Manchuria as a second supplement, which was officially announced at 1:00 PM this afternoon (6th Tongshen News Agency dispatch)

Judicial Yuan Interprets Ambiguous Clauses 37

(Nanjing) The Judicial Yuan, in response to a request from the President of the Jiangxi High Court for an interpretation of ambiguous clauses in Article 7 of the Emergency Law for Punishing Offenses Against the Republic of China, has provided the following interpretation: Regarding cases under the Emergency Law for Punishing Offenses Against the Republic of China, if the county had already transferred the accused person to the High Court or its branch for processing before the implementation of the law, and if the location of the High Court or its branch is a martial law zone, regardless of whether the county where the crime was committed is currently a martial law zone, a bandit suppression zone, or neither, after the implementation of the law, the court handling the case should transfer it to the highest military authority in its location for handling. FOREIGN TELEGRAMS

Gandhi Arrives in Paris from England, Speaks on Freedom and Peace 58

Havas, Paris, 6th: Gandhi delivered a speech in Paris yesterday to an extremely crowded audience. He stated that his desire is to see the nations of the world enjoy the blessings of peace and freedom. As for the art of governance, if it is based on virtue rather than force, it can achieve persuasion without destruction, which is the strongest, most effective, and most humane course of action in the world. He spoke of France's motto of liberty, equality, and fraternity, saying that France is commendable for practicing what it preaches. He also stated that his trip to England yielded nothing, but it is not impossible that the British people will feel our pain and change their minds in a short period of time. Therefore, hope is not yet lost.

Reuters, London, 5th: Gandhi, as usual, boarded a boat wearing coarse cloth today to cross the English Channel to tour Europe before returning to India. This afternoon, many British and Indian people saw him off at Victoria Station, many of whom were wearing the popular "Gandhi hats." Gandhi then traveled in third class to Folkestone. His parting words were: "If I must fight the people of England, it will not be out of resentment but out of love, and it will be like fighting with my dearest relatives. Therefore, I am determined to continue to cooperate to the best of my ability, and to measure it by what is suitable for national self-respect." When Gandhi boarded the boat to Boulogne at Folkestone, there was a large crowd watching, just as there had been when Gandhi landed at Dover a few weeks ago.

Havas, Paris, 5th: Gandhi, returning to India from England, passed through Paris and arrived here at 4:00 PM today. He will depart for Geneva at 8:30 AM tomorrow morning.

Havas, Rome, 5th: It is widely rumored here that Gandhi may take the opportunity of visiting Rome to meet with the Pope. The Catholic Church has a great deal of interest in India, and this statement seems credible.

United States' New Canal Between the Pacific and Atlantic 59

Extremely Important Militarily

National Society, Washington, 5th: US Army Chief of Staff Hurley published the Army Department's annual report, in which he stated that the Army Corps of Engineers had completed surveying a new canal to be dug in Nicaragua between the Pacific and Atlantic Oceans. Although there are currently fewer ships in the Panama Canal than in previous years, the new canal is extremely important militarily. He also gave a lengthy account of his inspection of the Philippines, but made no recommendations regarding the Filipinos' demands for independence.

Japanese Political Situation Will Not Shake 60

Prince Saionji Maintains the Status Quo

Dentsu, Tokyo, 6th: Interior Minister Adachi visited Prince Saionji at his villa in Okitsu to discuss the coalition cabinet problem. He returned to Tokyo yesterday at 5:00 PM. Unexpectedly, Prince Saionji considered the rapid advancement of this issue to be premature at this time and advocated maintaining the status quo. Therefore, the dark clouds looming over the political situation can be avoided.

Germany Denies Stopping Payment of Private Debts 61

National Society, Berlin, 5th: Today, German officials firmly denied the rumor that Germany intends to stop paying foreign private debts, which was fabricated by international speculators.

Soviet Russia's New Railway Opens to Traffic 62

Famous Church Demolished

Labor Mansion Rebuilt

National Society, Moscow, 5th: The new Soviet Russian railway line, built from the Altai Mountains to Kuznetsk, the new industrial hub of Siberia, opened to traffic on the 1st of this month. The line ends in Temirtau, the mining hub in the Altai Mountains, and its main purpose is to transport ore to Kuznetsk's smelters. Construction began three years ago. Due to the need to tunnel through several mountains and build six large bridges, the project was arduous but has now been completed. Reuters, Moscow, 6th: The famous Cathedral of Christ the Saviour here was destroyed by explosives today to build a giant labor mansion on its site. Architects from all over the world will compete for the design of the building. The cathedral was built in 1881 at a cost of 1.6 million English pounds to commemorate Napoleon's defeat. The artworks in the cathedral were removed and placed in various museums long ago.

NEWS

Situation of Japanese Troops Occupying West of Liao River 67

The Course of US Counselor's Inspection

Datushan Correspondence: The inspection delegation specially dispatched by the embassies of various countries in Peiping has already gathered in Jinzhou. The members of the delegation include: US Counselor Orde, British Consul Morse, Counselor Daranyi, Stewart, French Consul Rambiss, Air Force Attaché Fetter, Counselor Yankewei, German Councilor Curlebault, etc. Two representatives were elected by the whole country, one being US Counselor Orde and the other being German Councilor Curlebault. They departed by special train on the night of the 1st of this month to inspect the areas east of Datong Line and Datushan, where Chinese and Japanese troops had recently engaged in fierce fighting, as well as the west of the Liao River. Previously, the Northeast Commander's Office stationed in Jinzhou had specially dispatched a platoon of guards to protect the train, and Zhu Guangmu and Cai Yuan (currently the Director of the Finance Bureau of Peiping City) accompanied them to receive and entertain them. When the train arrived at Datushan, they split up. German Councilor Curlebault, accompanied by Zhu Guangmu and Cai Yuan, went to the Datong Line, turned back at Zhangwu, and returned to Jinzhou via Datushan by the original train at 11:00 PM on the 2nd. US Counselor Aldrich boarded a train from Datushan eastward at 5:30 AM on the 2nd. Fearing that it would cause a misunderstanding by the Japanese army, he left the guards at Datushan. Mr. Orde only took one guide. When the train reached Tangjiawopu Station, because Bridge No. 31 between Tangjiawopu and Lijiawopu was bombed and broken, he changed to the electric pressure car of the railway engineering office and proceeded to the bombed bridge to inspect it in detail. Only the length of the iron rail was intercepted, but the damage was very serious. He continued to Lijiawopu Station, where he saw several lines of black characters on the wall of the stationmaster's office room: "November 27, Showa 6, Japanese Empire 4th Brigade Infantry 5th Regiment 6th Company, 2nd Lieutenant Suzuki Hiroshi and 41 soldiers occupied, Japanese Empire Banzai, First Squad, Written by Yamaguchi." On the easternmost stone step of the station platform, there was a bomb crater left by a Japanese plane, about one foot deep. Outside the signaling post east of the station, Railway Bridge No. 32 was bombed and broken. On the bridge, there was an empty car No. 36 slightly leaning, with the front wheels suspended in the air and the rear wheels still on the rails. He continued for about two miles to Bridge No. 33, which was also bombed and broken. East of the bridge, there was a car from the railway engineering office in Huanggu Village with a material car. Next to it, there were two British engineers and fifty workers who were moving materials and equipment in preparation for repairing the bridge. With the permission of the engineer, Mr. Orde abandoned the electric pressure car and took the engineer's office car to the east. When he arrived at Raoyanghe Station, he learned that it was the site of fierce fighting that day, so he inspected it in detail. Railway Bridge No. 36, east of the platform, had been bombed and broken and has now been repaired. He boarded the train again and continued to Baiqibao Station. The stationmaster claimed that a Japanese troop train was coming from the previous station, so he stopped the train to wait. After about two hours, the troop train entered the station. There were a total of three cars in the train, one locomotive, one water tank, and one third-class South Manchurian car. There were 52 Japanese soldiers carrying four machine guns. After getting off the train, they acted as if they were searching. An officer spoke to Mr. Orde in English, claiming that there were too many bandits here, so they were specially dispatched to suppress them. At the same time, they cut off five telegraph wires as an excuse. Mr. Orde asked the stationmaster if there was any bandit alarm. The stationmaster replied that there were no bandits. This shows the ambition of the Japanese army, using bandit suppression as a cover. Mr. Orde carefully examined the machine guns carried by the Japanese army, which were made by the Fengtian Arsenal. Then, he boarded the train again and continued to Liuhegou Station and arrived at Xinmin. Mr. Orde got off the train and inspected the place in detail. There were about 300 Japanese soldiers stationed at the station and in the surrounding area and in various agencies in the city. They paid close attention to his actions, but did not interrogate him. A South Manchurian car was parked at the station (one locomotive, one water tank, and five passenger cars), with a Japanese stationmaster. Mr. Orde continued to Juliaohe Station. There was also a Japanese stationmaster at that station. East of the station is the Liao River Railway Bridge, with Japanese bunkers to the east of the bridge, surrounded by five rows of barbed wire, and 150 Japanese troops stationed there. After Mr. Orde finished inspecting, he boarded the train and returned to Xinmin. The train stopped at the station and Mr. Orde stayed in the car. At 5:00 AM on the 3rd, the original car returned to Raoyanghe and he transferred to the electric pressure car back to Tangjiawopu. He boarded the train back to Datushan at 9:50 AM and reported to Counselor Ma in Jinzhou by long-distance telephone. At 10:10 AM, Mr. Orde and the guards dispatched by the Commander's Office returned to Jinzhou by the original train. (December 4)

Peiping-Tianjin Reporter Group's Inspection Record of Raoyang 68

The Passage of the Japanese Army's Bombing of the Raoyang Area Peiping Correspondence: The Peiping-Tianjin Reporter Group's inspection team of twelve people left Peiping at 8:00 PM on the first of this month and arrived at Datushan Station at 6:00 PM on the second. On the third, they went to Lijiawopu, Raoyanghe, and Tangjiawopu to inspect. The findings of the investigation are recorded below.

The Jinzhou Provincial Government is Very Busy The reporter group boarded the Peiping-Nanjing Railway No. 101 passenger car and departed from Peiping at 8:00 PM on the first. At 11:20 PM that night, they arrived at Tianjin. Wang Fengrui, the chief of the engineering office of the Peiping-Nanjing Railway Bureau, was inspecting the details of the damage caused to the road by the Japanese army. He boarded the train with the Tianjin reporters from the old station and went east. In addition to the twelve members of the reporter group and the engineering personnel sent by the railway bureau to Guanwai, there were very few passengers. At 1:30 PM on the second, they arrived in Jinzhou. During the train's stop, the reporters got off the train and went to visit the Liaoning Provincial Government, which was located inside the Jiaotong University in Jinzhou. The reporters submitted their cards to Secretary-General Huang Jianqiu, who kindly received them. According to Huang, the local area of Jinzhou is still quite peaceful. All the affairs of the provincial government are being newly arranged, so they have been busy every day since its establishment two months ago. Up to now, all administrative matters have been roughly on track. A few days ago, the Japanese army suddenly advanced westward from Jiliuhe. At that time, the magistrate of Xinmin County was kidnapped by the Japanese army, but he managed to escape and has now arrived here. When the Japanese army attacked Raoyanghe, fortunately, our Zhongshan armored car prevented them from crossing west of Tangjiawopu. Thirteen Japanese planes and two armored trains bombed our armored car. Our armored car bravely responded and the Japanese army retreated. Although the Japanese army has not attacked westward in recent days, there are still four or five planes every day that come to reconnaissance around Goubangzi and Jinzhou. The Japanese army in Yingkou also crossed the river northward to Tianzhuangtai and Panshan to invade under the guise of target practice. Later, because the Japanese army on the Peiping-Nanjing Line withdrew, the Japanese army in that area also retreated to Yingkou. The reporters resigned and boarded the train eastward, arriving at Datushan at 6:00 PM.

Japanese Troop Train Comes to Patrol English Counselor Aldwell also arrived at Datushan on the morning of the second. He met with Section Chief Mao of that section and went east to inspect past Tangjiawopu. Because Bridges No. 31, 32, 33, and 36 were all bombed and destroyed, the train could not enter. He changed to a press-gate car to continue east. After stopping briefly at Lijiawopu, he continued east. At 2:00 PM, he arrived at Raoyanghe Station. He then split up to investigate. According to the investigation, a column of armored train and a column of troop train from Jiliuhe were ordered to advance westward on the morning of the 27th. In addition to carrying artillery, the two trains also carried machine gun teams, infantry, cavalry, etc., totaling more than 500 people. At 8:00 AM, they passed Baiqibao Station. The stationmaster of that station did not know that the Japanese army intended to attack, and in order to prevent danger from occurring on the road, he asked the Japanese troop train for a road pass. The Japanese soldiers ignored him and continued to drive east. The stationmaster of that station, seeing this situation, knew that the Japanese army's intentions were not good, and immediately sent telegrams to Raoyanghe and Lijiawopu stations to report the situation of the Japanese troop train without a road pass seizing the road to advance westward. (To be continued)

Part of the Japanese Illegal Pending Cases (1) 69

The Japanese had previously boasted of over three hundred pending cases. Our newspaper has tried to find and record the gist of them. In reality, what they call pending cases are only a few dozen cases, mostly based on strong-arming and unreasonable facts. The rest are trivial matters. Now, by comparing the Japanese illegal pending cases obtained from our investigation, the brutality and unreasonableness of the Japanese are clearly and firmly evidenced.

Summary of Pending Cases: Investigation of cases for which the Japanese government should be responsible but have not been resolved in recent years:

(1) Case of Withdrawal of Japanese Police from Japanese Consulates in China (Before the Unified Reign of the Qing Dynasty)

(2) Case of Japanese Warships Destroying Chinese Ships and Killing Chinese People Near Miao Street and Mazi (June, Year 9 of the Republic)

(3) Hunchun Case in Jilin (October 2, Year 9 of the Republic)

(4) Case of Japanese Man Ko Miyasaku Aiding Bandits and Disturbing the Border (September 24, Year 11 of the Republic)

(5) Case of Handover of Qingdao Observatory by Japanese Personnel (December, Year 11 of the Republic)

(6) Case of Revocation of South Manchurian Japanese Post Office (Year 11 of the Republic)

(7) June 1st Massacre in Changsha (June 1, Year 12 of the Republic)

(8) Massacre of Overseas Chinese in the Japanese Earthquake (September, Year 12 of the Republic)

(9) Case of Japan Not Purchasing Qingdao Salt According to Agreement (Year 15 of the Republic)

(10) First Korean Riot Case (December, Year 16 of the Republic)

(11) Case of Japanese or Taiwanese Selling Various Drugs (15 cases in total from Year 17 to Year 20 of the Republic)

(12) Case of Japanese Man Shigesumi Hosono's Negotiation on the Theory of Manchurian-Mongolian Administration (February, Year 17 of the Republic)

(13) Case of Japanese Warship "Tanikaze" Shooting and Killing Fishermen in Pingtan (February 27, Year 17 of the Republic)

(14) Case of Damage Caused by Qing Case (May 3, Year 17 of the Republic)

(15) Case of Japan Setting Up a Manchurian-Mongolian Pavilion at the Exposition (September, Year 17 of the Republic)

(16) Case of Japanese Fishing Boats Intrusion into Our Country's Territorial Waters to Fish (Year 18 of the Republic)

(17) Case of Japanese Brutally Killing Farmer Zhang Yutang in Gaiping County (May 23, Year 18 of the Republic)

(18) Case of Japanese Police Breaking into Liaoning Post Office and Stabbing Postal Workers (June 15, Year 18 of the Republic)

(19) Case of Japanese Regiment Trampling and Destroying Civilian Houses During Exercises in Changchun (August, Year 18 of the Republic)

(20) Case of Liaoning Japanese Police Beating Messenger He Youer (August 23, Year 18 of the Republic)

(21) Case of Tieling Japanese Soldiers Clashing with Police, Arbitrarily Arresting Security Team and Humiliating Them (September, Year 18 of the Republic)

(22) Case of Fuzhou Japanese Merchants Renting Land for Permanent Lease and Evading Land Tax (October, Year 18 of the Republic)

(23) Case of Shenyang Farmers Being Shot and Killed by Japanese Troops (October 17, Year 18 of the Republic)

(24) Case of Yanji Japanese Police Surrounding the Silin River Defense Corps Branch and Luring Teachers to Arrest (January 13, Year 19 of the Republic)

(25) Case of Japanese Ship "Toyumaru" Smuggling Military Supplies (February 23, Year 19 of the Republic)

(26) Case of Yanji Japanese Police Arresting Jin Rensan, Deputy Chairman of the Farmers' Association (April, Year 19 of the Republic)

(27) Case of Korean Smugglers Destroying the Andong Customs (May 17, Year 19 of the Republic)

(28) Case of Japanese Garrison Troops Shooting and Killing Vegetable Seller Ning Baomin Beside the South Manchurian Railway (June 2, Year 19 of the Republic)

(29) Case of Japanese Police Forcibly Seizing Smuggled Military Supplies at Andong Customs (June 3, Year 19 of the Republic)

(30) Case of Army Liaison Attached to the Longjing Village Army Company Being Beaten and Humiliated by Japanese Police for Arresting Gamblers (July 28, Year 19 of the Republic)

(31) Case of Fuzhou Japanese Consulate Arbitrarily Removing Opium Den Seals (August, Year 19 and March, Year 20 of the Republic)

(32) Case of Conflict Between Chinese and Japanese Military and Police in Longjing Village (October 6, Year 19 of the Republic)

(33) Case of Japanese Troops Pressuring the Andong City Electric Light Factory (April 28, Year 20 of the Republic)

(34) Case of Japanese Warships "Fuyong" and Others Sailing into Inland Rivers (May 18, Year 20 of the Republic)

(35) Case of Japanese Troops Forcibly Occupying Farmland in Linyu as a Target Practice Field (June, Year 20 of the Republic)

(36) Second Korean Riot Case (July, Year 20 of the Republic)

(38) Case of Changchun Japanese Police Taking the Pretext of Protecting Korean Farmers in Wanbaoshan and Entering the Inland (July, Year 20 of the Republic)

(39) Case of Japanese Military Exercises in the Tumen River (August, Year 20 of the Republic)

The case of withdrawing Japanese police from Japanese consulates in China: From the first year of the Xuantong reign of the Qing Dynasty, when China and Japan signed the Tumen River boundary treaty, Japanese consulates in the open trading ports of Yantou were equipped with one or two Japanese police officers. After the fourth year of the Republic, each of these Japanese consulates even added judicial police officers, up to twenty or thirty people. By the ninth year of the Republic, there were as many as 400 Japanese police officers stationed in the inland areas of Yanbian, causing repeated incidents. Negotiations with the Japanese consuls for withdrawal at any time were unsuccessful. Since the twelfth year of the Republic, Japanese police officers have also been found in the streets and stations of Harbin, and two police stations have been established, with a total of about 50 officers and police. Negotiations by the negotiators there have not resulted in withdrawal. Since the return of Qingdao to China, the Japanese consulate has also been equipped with more than 60 police officers who wear uniforms and carry knives, patrolling the streets. Negotiations for withdrawal have also been unsuccessful. Our side believes that the arbitrary establishment of Japanese police officers in Japanese consulates in China is a disregard for our country's administrative sovereignty, and we have repeatedly approved the consultation of the Northeast Political Affairs Committee to negotiate with the Japanese ambassador on May 30 of the 19th year to request immediate withdrawal. However, the Japanese side stated that the dispatch of these Japanese police officers is actually for full protection and to maintain Japanese residents. In order to avoid misunderstandings between Chinese officials and civilians, they will limit the wearing of uniforms except when necessary, but they do not mention the withdrawal at all.

Local Communication

Suzhou 70

Robbery cases frequently occur in the urban and rural areas of Wuxian County. Recently, robbery cases have been frequently reported in various cities and towns in Wuxian County. The water and land police are unable to quell them. In recent days, robbery cases have also occurred continuously in the urban area. A robbery case at Zhang Fushun Rice Store outside Jinmen had just occurred when a street robbery involving gold jewelry occurred at the entrance of Mitang Oil Mill the next day. On the same day, three bandits armed with weapons attempted to rob Xu Bangyu's home in Xijin Bridge. Fortunately, Xu escaped through the back door and shouted loudly for help. The bandits, realizing the situation was unfavorable, fled immediately. However, the bandits in various robbery cases all wore gray or yellow short clothes and had symbols. They were armed with pistols or Mauser pistols. The Public Security Bureau is trying to arrest them, but in reality, it feels very difficult. The County Chamber of Commerce has separately requested the responsible administrative and public security agencies to solve the case as soon as possible and pay close attention to prevention to ensure commercial security. The 60th Division stationed in Suzhou will jointly form a team with the county government, the Public Security Bureau, the Security Corps, and the Merchant Corps to investigate and deal with the situation in order to maintain local security.

Changshu 71

Another case against a party committee will be heard in court. Shi Minyong, the former supervisory committee member of the county party headquarters, was accused of fraud and financial embezzlement. The Wuxian District Court has repeatedly questioned him in court and acquitted Shi Minyong on the 4th of this month. Now, the executive committee member Shen Zuguang has repeatedly been accused by Gu Yushang, the former judge of this county, and Yao Yuren, a student from Shanghai University of Law and Politics, to the High Court for obstructing official duties. The Wudi Court had been designated to hold a hearing. Shen Zuguang believed that this case was a dispute over the previous murder case outside Ximen, which was a party action and not a personal matter. Therefore, he returned the summons to the plaintiffs and requested that the case be detained. Now, the Wudi Court has set the 10th of this month to hold a hearing for questioning. The summons has been sent to the county for delivery but has not been read. Whether Party Committee Member Shen will comply with the summons and appear in court this time is unknown.

Wuxi 72

Disputes over the silk factory trade union's audit of accounts. The silk factory industrial trade union in this county had not audited its finances for a long time, leading to many rumors in various factories. Therefore, it organized an economic audit committee to be responsible for the audit and appointed Wang Shihe, Chen Mengqi, Wang Xiubao, and other nine people as committee members. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, representatives from various factories held a joint meeting at the guild hall on the Bo'an to report the results of the audit to the general meeting. The audit committee reported that Hui Jizhi, the former managing director, had embezzled public funds. The entire venue was in an uproar. Subsequently, all the representatives decided to petition the county party headquarters and request: (1) Based on the audit committee's report, Hui Jizhi, the former managing director, had embezzled several thousand yuan through corruption. They requested his removal from office and investigation. (2) The memorial hall tarnished the funds given by the capitalists. Hui Jizhi took the liberty of transferring them to the construction of the guild hall. The construction cost of the guild hall was 27,000 yuan, but it has now been used up to 40,000 yuan. They requested an immediate investigation and the recovery of the wages borrowed from female workers in April. Li Deying and Wang Huilan were appointed as the chief representatives of the petition, and they, along with more than 100 representatives, went to the county party headquarters to petition. Wang Ciqing, the chief secretary, came out to meet them. Unexpectedly, Hua Guojun, He Wei, and others pretended to be petition representatives and privately submitted a petition, intending to confuse the situation. They were immediately exposed by Li Deying and others, the chief representatives of the petition. When they realized that their plan had been revealed, Hui Jizhi took back the petition. Chen Mengqi tried to snatch it back but was beaten by the other side. Fortunately, Wang Ciqing intervened and mediated, and the incident did not escalate. The petition representatives then stated their intentions. Comrade Wang promised to forward the petition to the committee members for review and asked them to submit a supplementary petition for discussion at a meeting.

Singing Tanhuang, Assaulting Police, and Seizing Guns. Liu Shide, the chief of the eighth branch of the Public Security Bureau of Zhouxin Town in the third district, had previously (on the 5th) received a report from Qian Qiwen, an official from the nearby 13th district office, stating that the continuous singing of flower drum Tanhuang in the Dongjia Bang area near Meng Lane in the district was harmful and vulgar. He requested that the police be dispatched to investigate and prohibit it. After receiving the report, Chief Liu dispatched police officer Pu Xia and 18 other police officers, including Liu Yuting, with guns to investigate and prohibit it at 8:00 PM that night. Unexpectedly, the villagers, upon seeing the police arrive, without asking any questions, shouted loudly and attacked. Seeing that the situation was unfavorable, the police fired warning shots into the sky to deter them. However, the villagers still did not disperse and seized a rifle held by police officer Liu Yuting. He was also severely injured in the head and waist. Zhu Fusheng was thrown into the river, and Zhang Guorui was injured in the right eye. Police officer Cao Xia was able to avoid the beating by hiding in the river. Police officer Cao and others escaped to the Chenlongcang Bridge area, hired a boat, and sent the injured police officer to the bureau for investigation. It was also reported that the leaders of this Tanhuang performance were the village head and the Tuzheng of the area. The County Public Security Bureau has ordered the arrest of the ringleaders to be sent to the County Court for interrogation.

Changzhou 73

Provincial order to borrow 80,000 yuan for water transport. The Wuyi County Government and the Finance Bureau received a provincial order to raise 80,000 yuan for winter water transport. Yesterday, they convened various township supervisors to discuss the matter. At that time, it was decided to allocate the amount according to the amount of silver taxed in each district, with each supervisor borrowing and raising funds to be paid in full by the 25th of this month. Orders were also issued to the district chiefs and township heads to assist in the process. In addition, the collection of taxes for the lower season this year has been open for a long time, but the amount collected is not strong. It has been decided to follow the rules of the deliberation plan in order to collect and remit taxes in advance.

A nephew strangled his uncle to death. Wu Shengbao of Changsheng Township in the fourth district of Wuyi County had a few acres of thin land and had no parents, wife, or children. The night before, he was suddenly strangled to death, and his body was moved and hung from the beam. When the villagers learned of this, they reported that the nearby security team had arrested three suspects, including Wu Tulin. Subsequently, the county court's supervising prosecutor went to the countryside to inspect the scene and confirmed that the strangulation was indeed the cause of death. The reason for the strangulation was that Shengbao intended to transfer his land to his daughter to inherit the property rights, so his nephews Tulin and others resorted to this cruel act. The supervising prosecutor is currently investigating the case.

Nantong 74

The Tonghai Customs brokerage firms are closed. The large-scale sales of coarse cloth from Tonghai County in the three northeastern provinces have been greatly affected by the loss of the customs outside the Pass this year. All the brokerage firms have now been closed, and the machine households in the four townships have also completely stopped weaving. Tongyi has always been centered on the cloth market, and the commercial market is currently in a state of desolation. The Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau has set up an office in Tong. The Ministry of Communications Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau has set up an office in Tong and appointed Shen Pixun as the director to handle ship registration and measurement affairs.

Yangzhou 75

An increase in vehicle fares led to a death. Zhu Shugui and his nephew Duanbao hired two rickshaws in front of Yunmen around 11:00 AM (on the 4th) to pull them to the Dashi Lane in the city to the home of Lu Ziqing at No. 18. The rickshaw pullers received 250 yuan each, but they felt it was insufficient and demanded an increase, which angered Zhu and others. They struck rickshaw puller Li Chuncheng (over 50 years old), causing his death. The other rickshaw puller, seeing that the situation was unfavorable, had already escaped. After Zhu and others killed Li, they asked the Lu family to have Xu Hengqing, a shop assistant from the Yixingsheng Rice Store next door, and Zhu Huaiyu, a shop assistant from the Chicken and Duck Shop, move the body to the Land Temple in the nearby Liansheng Lane. In an instant, the local people gathered to watch. It so happened that a relative of the deceased was also present and had seen the two shop assistants move the body. He immediately reported the incident to the police on duty, who reported it to the third sub-station of the Public Security Bureau, who in turn reported it to the court. The chief prosecutor, Zhu Ronggui, led the coroner to the scene. First, he summoned the deceased's wife, the perpetrators Zhu Shugui and Zhu Duanbao, the body movers Zhu Huaiyu and Xu Hengqing, and the related persons Lu Ziqing's mother-in-law Yao Bian, Lu Bian's maidservant Wang Chen, and Ma Hong, who lived with Lu, and other seven people for separate detention and interrogation. According to the perpetrators, Li's death was due to a self-inflicted fall. The coroner began the examination at 7:00 PM and found that the deceased had a scraped scalp on his forehead of about two inches, and his back of the head and waist were severely injured. After identification, it was confirmed that he had fallen to his death, and only the crime of moving the body by Zhu and others was to be prosecuted. The deceased's son, Deju, learned of the situation and rushed to request a re-examination, saying that his father had indeed been beaten to death. Chief Zhu immediately approved the re-examination. The results showed that there was a knife wound on the forehead and a hole in the back of the head, confirming that he had been beaten to death. He immediately instructed the Zhen Ding to guard the body, and the police took Zhu Shugui, Zhu Duanbao, the body movers Zhu Huaiyu and Xu Hengqing, and the related persons Lu Bian, Wang Chen, and other six people to the court for detention pending investigation.

Huzhou 76

The notorious bandit Cheng Mingyi, who escaped, was recaptured and robbed Shiwanzhen and hijacked the Xinjia Ban steamer. The notorious bandit Cheng Mingyi, who robbed Shiwanzhen and hijacked the Xinjia Ban steamer, was arrested by Captain Wang of the 13th Water Army Team last month. After being interrogated by the city's Qingxiang Bureau, he was detained in the County Public Security Bureau. A few days ago, the bandit escaped over the wall from the detention center. Chen Tiemin, the head of the Shicong Security Corps, learned that the bandit had fled from prison and was hiding in the Zongguan Temple near Lujiawan. The corps head secretly wrote to Pan Shuren, the director of the Wuxing County Public Security Bureau. After learning of the situation, Director Pan immediately sent many police officers to the area to join forces with the local security corps members. They went to the temple at 5:00 AM on the 3rd and found the bandit and a woman sleeping together. They were arrested and taken back to Huzhou for interrogation.

Shangyu 77

A kidnapping case occurred in Shenjia Village. Shen Jiahai, a resident of Shenjia Village, Tangban, which borders Yu and Sheng counties, works in Nanjing. He has a mother, wife, and two young children at home. Unexpectedly, more than 20 bandits suddenly broke down the door and went upstairs a few days ago. Jiahai's eldest son heard the alarm and hid behind the bed. The bandits were disappointed and set the house on fire. Jiahai's eldest son was shocked and suddenly ran out from behind the bed, attracting the attention of the bandits, who seized him and carried him away. When the villagers learned of the situation, they chased after the bandits, but they had already gone far away. The fire in the side house was first extinguished by the villagers, preventing a major disaster.

Important Educational News

Peking University Students' Demonstration Delegation Demonstrates in Beijing 78

Zhang Wenyou, Liu Songyun, Wang Rongcheng, Wang Yuquan, and Fang Zhenyue, members of the Peking University Students' Demonstration Delegation, arrived in Shanghai yesterday and reported on the situation of the demonstration in Beijing as follows:

More than 300 members of the Peking University Students' Demonstration Delegation arrived in Nanjing and stayed in the Central University Gymnasium. After arriving in Beijing, the delegation contacted various parties and invited reporters from various newspapers and news agencies to report on the purpose of the Nanjing demonstration and the journey south. Fearing that the true situation would not be understood by all parties, the delegation sent representatives Zhang Baichuan and others to the Garrison Headquarters to report on all the procedures and routes of the demonstration before the demonstration began, and submitted a written statement to the authorities for understanding. However, the representatives did not return after going at 8:00 AM. It was not until around 11:00 AM that they had not returned. Soon, the delegation received a report from another party that the representatives who had gone to the Garrison Headquarters had been detained by the authorities. The students in the delegation were extremely angry at the time and immediately decided to have all groups and teams line up and set off for the demonstration in turn. The order was still good at the time. In addition to shouting slogans along the way after departure, the students all held small flags with slogans such as "Down with Japanese Imperialism" and "Oppose the Traitorous Government." Many students from Central University also expressed their sympathy. The delegation set off from Central University. Not far after leaving the gate, there were many police officers stationed on both sides of Chengxian Street. As the large team moved forward, the police and military police suddenly stepped forward to stop them. The propaganda team of the delegation was at the front of the team at the time, and two or three people were immediately arrested by the military police. Yue Zengyu, the commander of the large team, immediately ordered the team to stop moving forward and explained the significance of the demonstration to the military police. However, while the two sides were negotiating, five or six hundred military police officers arrived from the rear of the team and surrounded the entire team and arrested the students. The order was disrupted for a while. Because the students were surrounded from the front and back, some of them climbed over the short walls beside the street and escaped. However, there were too many military police officers, and although the students resisted slightly, no less than seventy or eighty people were injured in the chaos, including more than ten seriously injured, including one female student. Because of the panic, she fell into a ditch and was severely injured by being hit with stones from both sides. It is estimated that about 200 people were arrested by the military police at that time, including about thirty or forty female students. The escaped students all returned to Central University one after another. Except for those who were missing, there were more than seventy people remaining. After receiving the news, all the students of Central University were extremely angry and immediately convened a general meeting of all students to decide to assist the Peking University students and gathered more than 1,000 students from Central University and Peking University to go to the Garrison Headquarters under the command of the demonstration delegation and demand the immediate release of the Peking University classmates and other conditions. By 10:00 PM, the authorities had escorted the arrested students to Xiaolingwei for detention. After hearing the news, various schools in Nanjing sent representatives to express their condolences, but they were all rejected. This morning (the 6th), all the schools went to the National Government again. At the same time, the Peking University students received a telegram from the third batch of representatives of the Peking University demonstration delegation to Beijing, saying that all the students had decided to go to Beijing within days to provide assistance. The delegation also sent representatives to Shanghai to ask for assistance from various groups in Shanghai.

Local

The Intention of the Public Works Department to Revise the Regulations on Subsidizing Private Chinese Schools 79

丨Published by the Information Office of the Public Works Department丨

Focusing on the point of ethnic hatred

The Information Office of the Public Works Department released a message yesterday as follows:

The Public Works Department hopes that private Chinese schools in the Public Concession should be made as consistent as possible with the methods of schools in various districts. Chinese children's schools not established by the Public Works Department in the Concession are almost entirely managed by the Chinese themselves. Except for the special circumstances of the Concession, they have never been subject to any restrictions. According to Chinese law, the power of jurisdiction actually lies with the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education. The Public Works Department recognizes both of these points. Therefore, the Public Works Department has proposed to the Mayor of Shanghai that the Bureau accepts the recommendation of the Bureau of Education to show that private schools are qualified for subsidy fees. If the Bureau of Education assumes this responsibility, 丨we hope that the Bureau will be willing to assume it,丨 the allocation and distribution of this subsidy fee will be jointly handled by the Public Works Department and the Bureau of Education, based on the report of the Chinese Committee Branch of the Education Committee of the Public Works Department and the recently approved regulations. These regulations are called "General Conditions for Chinese Schools," and their content is the same as those set by the Public Works Department for private foreign children's schools, except that the scope of implementation of the two is different.

At the beginning of this year, the Public Works Department approved the listing of 150,000 taels of silver in the budget for subsidy fees for private schools. This amount has been approved by the annual meeting of taxpayers, but it has not yet been actually spent.

The Education Committee of the Public Works Department carefully considered the regulations on subsidy fees during drafting and translation to ensure that the meaning of the Chinese and English texts was consistent. Among them, there was originally a section on the curriculum outline, which caused great difficulty. There was concern that this would cause misunderstandings on the Chinese side. Therefore, after full discussion by the Education Committee, it was unanimously advocated to participate in the revision and modify this section as follows:

Article 10, Clause B: Each school should encourage students to love the country and be good citizens. Anything in the curriculum that is sufficient to hurt national feelings and cause ethnic hatred must not be used.

This amendment has been approved by the Public Works Department.

During the discussion in the Education Committee, it was stated that this clause on prohibiting curricula that are prone to cause ethnic hatred was drafted before the current political situation occurred. Therefore, this provision has absolutely nothing to do with the current situation of estrangement between the two ethnic groups in the Concession. Moreover, the Public Works Department has absolutely no intention of interfering excessively with Chinese schools. Because the Public Works Department is an administrative body in a large urban area, it is its responsibility to provide subsidy fees to private schools, and it has absolutely no intention of prohibiting patriotic actions in these schools. The Chairman of the Education Committee further stated that the establishment of this prohibition clause is because the schools are located in the international Public Concession. Therefore, the curriculum should be based on promoting international cooperation and friendship. Even in the current tense situation, the Education Committee has a good opportunity to show that patriotic actions in schools do not necessarily cause ethnic resentment. He believes that it is possible to guide children to love the country in schools without causing them to hate another ethnic group in the Concession. (To be continued)

Yesterday, the Anti-Japanese Joint Conference of Middle School Students Decided to Strike 80

The representative meeting will be held again at 1:00 PM today. The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Joint Conference of middle school students in this city held its sixth emergency representative meeting at the conference office yesterday afternoon. Thirty-five schools attended. The chairman group elected by public vote was Hui Ling, Li Bin Gongshi, Chen Liyan (Zhengfeng), and Fang Mo recorded Sun Yucai (Jingye) to start the meeting with the usual ceremonies. The resolutions are as follows: (1) The resolution to implement a general strike in middle schools from the 7th was passed. (2) In view of the tense situation, the conference should hold a joint meeting of the executive committees with the university joint association to make a decision on unified action. (Resolution) Passed. (3) To unite all sectors of the country to implement strikes, market strikes, work strikes, and tax strikes in order to urge the government to send troops to resist Japan. (Resolution) Passed. (4) Implementing large-scale demonstration movements. (Resolution) To be submitted to the joint meeting of universities and middle schools for detailed discussion. (5) How the conference should express the national crisis in each school's strike case. (Resolution) Reserved and will be discussed at the representative meeting tomorrow. (6) The meeting time of the conference has been long, and it should be temporarily adjourned. It will be continued tomorrow (i.e., the 7th) at 1:00 PM at the senior high school department of Shanghai High School for a meeting and discussion. (Resolution) Passed. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

China Maintains Fourth Year of Victory in International Race Walking Competition 85

China Wins Both Team and Individual Championships, England Second, France Third

Champion Shi Jinsheng Sets New Record at Two Hours, Twenty-Seven Minutes, and Three Seconds

Shi Jinsheng, Hou Genren, Zhou Ruquan, and Xie Xingdao of the Chinese race walking team, amidst cheers from tens of thousands of people yesterday, defeated the British team again and maintained the fourth year of the International Race Walking Championship. Shi Jinsheng set a new record by walking this long 17-mile and 100-yard course in two hours, twenty-seven minutes, and three seconds. The grandstand of the Racecourse was packed with men, women, old, and young, and the spectators along the way were also thronged. This year's grand occasion was the greatest. The Chinese team scored fourteen points, with the British team in second place with twenty-five points, and the French team in third place with fifty-two points. The Irish and Russian teams did not have their fourth team member arrive and were not counted.

Record Breaking 87

| Overthrowing the record set by Yang in 1929

| 2 hours 29 minutes 53.8 seconds record

Shi Jinsheng's hard training throughout the year has resulted in rapid progress. He once set an astonishing record of 2 hours and 19 minutes during the trial run. Although he did not achieve his best result yesterday, he has overthrown the record of 2 hours 29 minutes 53.8 seconds set by the Englishman Yang in 1929. Shi's time of 2 hours 27 minutes 03 seconds has become a new record.

The Course of the Struggle 88

Shi Jinsheng always at the forefront

Champion Shi Jinsheng not only set a new record, but also remained in the lead from beginning to end. Of the more than fifty participants, only their backs could be seen. The second place was almost a mile behind, which is extremely rare.

Firing the gun and taking the lead

At 7:50, sixty-four athletes lined up in numerical order at the intersection of Carter Road. The four members of the Chinese team were in the far left corner. After roll call and arrangement, as Besley's gun fired, more than sixty pairs of flying feet started simultaneously. Shi Jinsheng and Hou Genren took the lead, heading towards Jing'an Temple, followed by Niugebao, Shipon, Kim, France, and Xie Xingdao.

Three abreast in front of Jing'an Temple

Arriving in front of Jing'an Temple, only one mile had passed. Shi Jinsheng, Niugebao, and Davis were running abreast. Fifty yards behind were Zhou Ruquan, Xie Xingdao, France, Shipon, Kim, Zhang Luzhou, Xi Lieteng, Qi Miyaning, Losi, and Hou Genren.

Gradually separating before Zhaofeng Garden

Passing Gexifei Road and reaching Xianglinan Road, passing in front of Zhaofeng Garden, the distance was three and a half miles. At that time, it was 8:20, and the positions of each person gradually became uneven. Niugebao was closely following Shi Jinsheng. Seventy yards behind, the Englishman France shrugged and advanced another thirty yards. Xie Xingdao and Zhou Ruquan came side by side, Kim, Davis, and Shipon were twenty yards further back, and Hou Genren was even further behind.

Taking the lead on Robegen Road

Along the Suzhou River, advancing in the previous formation, turning into Robegen Road, approaching the intersection of Lincoln Road, the distance was six miles, accounting for one-third of the entire course. Shi Jinsheng had already dropped Niugebao and taken the lead. Niugebao was one hundred yards behind Shi, and France was two hundred yards behind Shi. Zhou and Xie were still running side by side fifty yards away, Kim, Davis, and Shipon followed closely, and Hou Genren was still behind.

Tense situation on Hongqiao Road

After Robegen Road, turning west onto Hongqiao Road, eight miles had already been covered. At that time, the Chinese and British teams were competing fiercely, and it was difficult to predict the outcome. Zhou Ruquan had already overtaken Xie Xingdao on Robegen Road. Shi Jinsheng was still in the lead. Excluding Niugebao, the second place was France, one hundred and twenty yards away. Zhou and Xie were fifty yards apart, and Kim and Davis were eighty yards behind. Hou Genren caught up with Shipon, only five or six yards behind Davis.

Separately calculated, the Chinese team occupied the 1st, 3rd, 4th, and 7th positions, while the British team occupied the 2nd, 5th, 6th, and 8th.

Hou sped up at Jiaotong University

On Hongqiao Road, Hou Genren accelerated and overtook Davis. Passing Jiaotong University to Haige Road, Hou again overtook Davis, trailing Xie Xingdao by thirty yards. This was twelve miles, one-third away from the finish line. Hou's efforts were key to victory. At Lafayette Road and Albert Road, Hou again overtook France, trailing Kim and ranking fourth. At Weihaiwei Road, he surpassed Kim and Zhou Ruquan, competing with Niugebao. Hou's efforts to accelerate were for the honor of the country.

Champion enters the arena to thunderous applause

Hou Genren's catch-up greatly increased the Chinese team's hope. Shi Jinsheng's first place was no longer in doubt. At around 10:27, Shi Jinsheng entered the arena amidst thunderous applause. Niugebao and Hou Genren followed one mile later, with Hou ultimately losing to Niugebao by a few steps, which was a pity. Zhou Ruquan was thirty yards behind in third place, followed by the Englishman Kim, etc. Xie Xingdao was ranked tenth. The Chinese team won the championship with fourteen points, retaining the title for the fourth time.

Silk and Tea: Last week, there was still no turning point in the silk market 99

Overseas actual sales are not moving... hoarders suppress prices and hoard

The provincial order requires silk factories to resume work... Manufacturers sell at a loss

Last week, there was still no turning point in the local foreign silk market. It was found that the actual sales of Lyon Hua Silk were not moving. Although the silk in London was thin, the economic situation was unstable. Silk merchants had no appetite for silk. The price of New York Japanese silk was cheap. Grade B white factory was 80 to 85 points. Yivannais telegram turned the price to only 800 to 834 taels. British hoarders took the opportunity to suppress prices and hoard endlessly. The five or six hundred packages of grade B white factory warp imported by Jardine Matheson, etc., initially opened at 834 taels, and then fell to 800 taels. The provincial order required silk factories that received silk public bonds to not stop production without reason. Those who have stopped work should immediately find ways to resume work to maintain the lives of workers. Each manufacturer needs funds for resumption of work, and it is difficult to deposit silk goods (the silk quota worth one thousand taels can only be obtained for four or five hundred taels). They had no choice but to sell at a discount. However, the loss was too great (the selling price of 800 taels per package was at least more than 200 taels). Therefore, the negotiations were still in progress last Friday and could not be fully signed and recorded. Last week, more than 500 packages of spot silk were exported, and 600 to 700 packages of spot and futures silk were traded. The price of overseas Hua Silk was still weak. Local News

Wang Jingwei Meets with Representatives of Capital Schools 102

Mr. Wang has instructions at Guandulu on Gordon Road

More than one hundred and eighty representatives of students from various schools in the capital arrived in Shanghai the night before. Yesterday morning, they sent seven representatives to the French Concession to visit Mr. Wang. It was agreed to meet all the representatives at Wu's Mansion, Guandulu, Gordon Road at 2:00 pm. The representatives were transferred to several teams by car, but due to insufficient vehicles, they did not arrive until 3:30 pm. Mr. Wang served tea and snacks. At 4:00 pm, the meeting began. After the commander-in-chief of the delegation, Wang Jianyu, explained the mission of coming to Shanghai, Mr. Wang delivered instructions until 5:00 pm. The letter of welcome from the representatives and Mr. Wang's instructions are recorded below.

Welcome Petition: Presenting the matter of welcoming Mr. Wang to Beijing to preside over the party and the country's major plans. I believe that the party and the country are unfortunately in successive disasters, and floods are rampant in the past. The Japanese pirates are rampant in the future. The people are already suffering from natural disasters, and the country is being invaded by whales. The rebellious flames are becoming more and more intense, and the people's hearts are panicked. The discord between Ning and Yue is difficult to achieve peace. If this continues, the country will perish without a day. Mr. Wang is an advanced leader of the revolution and leads the masses. He advocates people's governance to correct the malpractices of the times and to elaborate on people's rights. He is indignant at the imminent national crisis and embraces peace to seek unity. Our group is happy to follow. I dare to ask you to consider the difficulties of the times, to follow the public opinion, to promote the realization of peace in the shortest possible time, and to preside over the party and government in Beijing as soon as possible, to correct the accumulated malpractices of the past, to revitalize the spirit of party governance, to vigorously implement revolutionary diplomacy, and to recover the lost land in the Northeast. The capital people swear to be Mr. Wang's backing, and the people of the whole country will be directed by Mr. Wang. I urge you to be aware of this. Respectfully present to the revolutionary leader Mr. Wang.

Mr. Wang Jingwei meets with representatives of Beijing schools and takes a photo (taken by this museum) 103

Mr. Wang's instructions: After the commander-in-chief of the delegation, Wang Jianyu, stated the purpose of coming to Shanghai to petition, Mr. Wang gave instructions: "Dear representatives, I feel very uneasy in my heart that you have traveled all the way from Nanjing to Shanghai. I originally wanted to entertain you at my house, but because the place is too shallow, I borrowed Wu's Mansion to meet you. The last Shanghai Peace Conference was also held here. I met with representatives of various groups in Shanghai every day. Today, I can meet with you again. Although the place is still not enough, I really want to take this opportunity to express my respect for you. I came to Shanghai this time to share the difficulties of the country. Let's look at the history of the world in the past two hundred years. In these two hundred years, I don't know how many countries in the world have perished. However, at the same time, I don't know how many countries have been able to struggle to survive despite suffering all kinds of oppression. Now China is being invaded and oppressed by Japan. Many people think that China cannot resist Japan and hold infinite pessimism about national affairs. But is this attitude right? Let's look at the history of various countries in the world. Which country has not experienced a dangerous period? For example, during the Franco-Prussian War in 1871, France was in danger of perishing at any time. The uniforms of the volunteer army are exactly the same as the volunteer army of the French people at that time. Because the French people were able to work hard, France was finally saved. Moreover, since that time, France has no longer had the struggle between the imperial system and the republic, nor the terror of Louis' restoration and Napoleon's revival of the imperial system. Now France is still a strong country in the world. Let's look at the Great Revolution in our country in the seventh year of the Republic of China. At that time, Germany took advantage of its victory and negotiated peace with Russia. The Russian government signed a humiliating peace treaty. Many people thought that Russia would perish. The Russian revolution also failed from then on. But the fact is not. Because the Russian people can fight together, Russia still survives in the world. We can also look at Germany in the eighth year of the Republic of China. At that time, after Germany was defeated, it was subjected to all kinds of oppression from various countries and was in danger of perishing at any time. But because the German people persevered and struggled, Germany was finally saved. In this way, although China is now in a dangerous period, we must have a way to save the country. However, the way to save the country must be automatically thought out by the people. This is the real way. But now there are some people who say that if the current Kuomintang government declares war on Japan and is defeated, the Kuomintang will perish. Otherwise, if the Kuomintang negotiates peace with Japan, it can be accused of selling out the country and will also perish. But those who say these words will never do so if they are patriotic people. Because when the country is in trouble, no one should use diplomacy to deal with internal affairs. So to the outside of the party, so to the party, just as a faction of comrades who work with the brothers have always opposed the Nanjing government, but from beginning to end they have opposed the Nanjing government in order to realize the fifth political system. They will never use the problem of diplomacy as a tool for internal struggle. As for the current diplomatic methods, I think there are eight words: "Resist on the one hand and negotiate on the other." We must know that Japan's dispatch of troops this time is not tolerated by the international community. On the one hand, it violates the League of Nations, and on the other hand, it violates the Non-War Pact. I remember that during the war between Germany and France in the third year of the Republic of China, Germany's dispatch of troops passed through Belgium and destroyed Belgium's neutrality, so Britain came to attack Germany. Moreover, Japan's dispatch of troops to the Northeast this time is even more unreasonable than Germany's dispatch of troops to Belgium. Therefore, for the sake of their own national glory and for the sake of maintaining world peace, all countries must intervene. But if China declares war on Japan, the situation will be different. They can all remain neutral. It should be noted that not declaring war does not mean not resisting. Japan's actions this time are like robbers openly robbing. If we encounter robbers breaking into the house, the only way is to face him head-on while ringing the alarm to cooperate in catching them. Therefore, I advocate that we must resist on the one hand and negotiate on the other. If we can do so, we will not be absolutely disappointed. The current organization of volunteer troops everywhere is an expression of working together to overcome the difficulties of the country. Some people think that the current volunteer troops are not well trained and have insufficient guns. How can they be helpful? In fact, this is not the case. Because although the volunteer troops are not perfect in material terms, their spirit is very valuable. At least, it must be able to arouse the attention of the people of the whole country and make them all have the determination to resist by force. If this is the case, the country will definitely be able to have the final rescue. Regarding the establishment of a neutral zone in Jinzhou and the joint management of Tianjin, I remember that at the time of the Peace Conference, there were diplomatic principles and policies that were agreed upon by both parties and negotiated by the Nanjing government. Therefore, after I heard the news that a neutral zone was established in Jinzhou and a joint management area in Tianjin, I immediately sent a telegram to Nanjing to inquire. Although I have not received a reply to this day, Mr. He Jingzhi and Mr. Shao Lizi came to Shanghai from Nanjing today to explain this matter. It is said that there is no such thing as establishing a neutral zone in Jinzhou and jointly managing Tianjin, so we can rest assured. Regarding my trip to Nanjing, this may be realized in the near future. Originally, after the Peace Conference, everyone decided to send Sun, Li, and Chen back to Guangdong, and I, Wu, and Zou would stay in Shanghai to wait for the future results. Now the Fourth National Congresses of Nanjing and Guangzhou have elected the Fourth Central Committee members. The Shanghai delegates have also completed the election. Now we are only waiting for them to arrive from Guangzhou, then I can go to Nanjing with them. Our purpose in going to Nanjing is to share the difficulties of the country externally and to realize democratic politics internally. Sharing the difficulties of the country and realizing democratic politics is actually only one thing. Because only with democratic politics can the people have the possibility of sharing the difficulties of the country. Now the comrades in Guangzhou are about to set off tomorrow and will arrive in Shanghai in a few days. Then the date when I meet you in Nanjing will not be far away. Today, I fully accept your enthusiasm for coming to Shanghai this time and express my deepest respect to you."
